  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 1. AUTH + API LAYER
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function getToken() {
    for (const store of [localStorage, sessionStorage]) {
      try {
        for (const key of ['access_token', 'token', 'id_token', 'auth_token']) {
          const v = store.getItem(key);
          if (v && v.length > 20) return v;
        }
      } catch (_) {}
    }
    return null;
  }

  let _sessionId = null;

  function captureSessionId() {
    if (_sessionId) return;
    // Check storage first for a numeric session/shift value
    for (const store of [localStorage, sessionStorage]) {
      try {
        for (let i = 0; i < store.length; i++) {
          const key = store.key(i);
          const val = store.getItem(key);
          if (
            key &&
            (key.toLowerCase().includes('session') || key.toLowerCase().includes('shift')) &&
            val &&
            /^\d+$/.test(val.trim())
          ) {
            _sessionId = val.trim();
            return;
          }
        }
      } catch (_) {}
    }
    // Intercept the next Angular XHR to steal x-session-id from its headers
    if (!window._mpkXHRPatched) {
      window._mpkXHRPatched = true;
      const origSet = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.setRequestHeader;
      XMLHttpRequest.prototype.setRequestHeader = function (name, value) {
        if (name.toLowerCase() === 'x-session-id' && value && !_sessionId) {
          _sessionId = String(value);
          XMLHttpRequest.prototype.setRequestHeader = origSet;
          window._mpkXHRPatched = false;
        }
        return origSet.call(this, name, value);
      };
    }
  }

  function mkHeaders(extra = {}) {
    const h = {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      Accept: 'application/json',
      Authorization: `Bearer ${getToken()}`,
      'x-warehouse-id': String(WAREHOUSE_ID),
      ...extra,
    };
    if (_sessionId) h['x-session-id'] = _sessionId;
    return h;
  }

  async function waitForSession() {
    if (_sessionId) return;
    captureSessionId();
    // Short poll - pre-warm at boot means this rarely needs to wait
    for (let i = 0; i < 5 && !_sessionId; i++) {
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));
    }
  }

  async function apiGet(path) {
    await waitForSession();
    const res = await fetch(API_BASE + path, { method: 'GET', headers: mkHeaders() });
    if (res.status === 401) {
      _showSessionExpired();
      throw new Error('Session expired');
    }
    if (!res.ok) {
      const body = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
      throw new Error(`${body.message || `API error ${res.status}`} [${res.status}]`);
    }
    return res.json();
  }

  async function apiPost(path, data) {
    await waitForSession();
    const res = await fetch(API_BASE + path, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: mkHeaders(),
      body: JSON.stringify(data),
    });
    if (res.status === 401) {
      _showSessionExpired();
      throw new Error('Session expired');
    }
    if (!res.ok) {
      const body = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
      throw new Error(body.message || `API error ${res.status}`);
    }
    return res.json();
  }

  // Fire-and-forget job unassign - called when picker backs out of summary
  function unassignJob(jobId) {
    if (!jobId) return;
    console.log('[MalpaPick] unassigning job', jobId);
    apiGet(`job/job/unassign-job&job_id=${jobId}`)
      .catch(e => console.warn('[MalpaPick] unassign-job failed:', e.message));
  }

  // -- Pick resume state (sessionStorage) --------------------------------------
  const _RESUME_KEY = 'mpk_resume';

  function savePickResumeState() {
    if (!State.jobId || !State.profile || !State.instruction) return;
    try {
      const snapshot = {
        profileId:            State.profile.id,
        jobId:                State.jobId,
        instructionId:        State.instruction.id,
        pickProgressCurrent:  State.pickProgress?.current || 1,
        pickProgressTotal:    State.pickProgress?.total   || 1,
        containersByPosition: State.containersByPosition,
        savedAt:              Date.now(),
      };
      sessionStorage.setItem(_RESUME_KEY, JSON.stringify(snapshot));
      console.log('[MalpaPick] pick state saved for resume');
    } catch(e) {
      console.warn('[MalpaPick] savePickResumeState failed:', e.message);
    }
  }

  function clearPickResumeState() {
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem(_RESUME_KEY); } catch(_) {}
  }

  function loadPickResumeState() {
    try {
      const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(_RESUME_KEY);
      if (!raw) return null;
      const s = JSON.parse(raw);
      // Discard if older than 8 hours
      if (Date.now() - (s.savedAt || 0) > 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000) {
        clearPickResumeState();
        return null;
      }
      return s;
    } catch(_) { return null; }
  }

  // Session expiry - show a clear banner over whatever screen is active
  let _sessionExpiredShown = false;
  function _showSessionExpired() {
    if (_sessionExpiredShown) return;
    _sessionExpiredShown = true;
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;
    // Overlay the current screen
    const banner = document.createElement('div');
    banner.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute;inset:0;z-index:9999;background:rgba(0,0,0,.75)',
      'display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center',
      'padding:24px;gap:16px;text-align:center',
    ].join(';');
    banner.innerHTML = `
      <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:#fff">LOCKED</div>
      <div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:#fff">Session Expired</div>
      <div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);line-height:1.5">
        Your C7 session has timed out.<br>Please log back in to continue picking.
      </div>
      <button id="mpk-session-dismiss" style="
        margin-top:8px;padding:12px 24px;background:#20a8d8;color:#fff;
        border:none;font-size:15px;font-weight:600;font-family:Roboto,sans-serif;
        cursor:pointer;border-radius:4px;
      ">Dismiss</button>`;
    root.style.position = 'relative';
    root.appendChild(banner);
    document.getElementById('mpk-session-dismiss')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      banner.remove();
      _sessionExpiredShown = false;
      State.reset();
      renderProfileSelect();
    });
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 2. STATE STORE
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  const State = {
    screen: 'PROFILE_SELECT',
    profile: null,
    jobId: null,
    instruction: null,
    groupRecord: null,
    summary: null,
    containersByPosition: {},
    scanCount: 0,
    reasons: [],
    containerTypes: [],
    profiles: [],
    pickProgress: null,      // { current, total }
    voiceEnabled: (() => {
      try { const v = sessionStorage.getItem('mpk_voice'); return v === null ? true : v === '1'; }
      catch(_) { return true; }
    })(),  // persists for browser session
    allInstructions: [],     // cached from summary fetchJobInstructions call
    barcodeMap: {},          // barcode -> instruction_id lookup, built at accept
    containerPrefixes: [],   // valid container prefixes for O(1) validation

    reset() {
      this.screen = 'PROFILE_SELECT';
      // profile intentionally NOT reset -- persists selection for next job
      this.jobId = null;
      this.instruction = null;
      this.groupRecord = null;
      this.summary = null;
      this.containersByPosition = {};
      this.scanCount = 0;
      this.pickProgress = null;
      // note: voiceEnabled intentionally NOT reset - persists across jobs
      this.allInstructions = [];
      this.barcodeMap = {};
      this.containerPrefixes = [];
    },
  };

  // DOM references - populated by buildShell() and renderXxx() functions
  let R = {};

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 4. NAV INJECTION
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  let _navClickAttached = false;

  function _attachNavClickListener() {
    if (_navClickAttached) return;
    _navClickAttached = true;
    // Capture phase - fires before Angular can intercept the click
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      const nav = document.getElementById('mpk-nav');
      if (!nav) return;
      if (nav === e.target || nav.contains(e.target)) openPick();
    }, true);
  }

  let _initDataPrefetched = false;
  function injectNav() {
    _attachNavClickListener();
    if (document.getElementById('mpk-nav')) return;
    const ul = document.querySelector('div.sidebar nav ul.nav');
    if (!ul) return;

    const li = document.createElement('li');
    li.id = 'mpk-nav-li';
    li.className = 'nav-item ng-star-inserted';

    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.id = 'mpk-nav';
    a.className = 'nav-link ng-star-inserted';
    a.setAttribute('href', 'javascript:void(0)');

    // Same Malpa logo image as Pack v3 - onerror hides it gracefully if CDN unavailable
    // Logo embedded as base64 - no external URL dependency

    li.appendChild(a);
    ul.insertBefore(li, ul.firstChild); // Top of sidebar

    // Background prefetch - profiles/types/reasons load while user is still on C7
    // By the time they tap the nav, the dropdown is instant
    if (!_initDataPrefetched) {
      _initDataPrefetched = true;
      setTimeout(() => initData(), 500); // small delay to let C7 settle first
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 5. SHELL / TAB BUILD
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function measureHeight() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view');
    if (!panel) return;
    // Use window.innerHeight minus the panel's top offset
    // This gives the actual visible height regardless of C7's container layout
    const rect      = panel.getBoundingClientRect();
    const available = Math.floor(window.innerHeight - rect.top);
    if (available > 100) {
      panel.style.height     = available + 'px';
      panel.style.maxHeight  = available + 'px';
      panel.style.minHeight  = available + 'px';
    }
  }

  function buildShell() {
    if (document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view')) return; // double-open guard

    const tabBar     = document.querySelector('ul.nav.nav-tabs[role="tablist"]');
    const tabContent = document.querySelector('div.tab-content');
    if (!tabBar || !tabContent) {
      console.warn('[MalpaPick] Could not find C7 tab bar or tab content.');
      return;
    }

    // Store currently active tab + panel so we can restore exactly on close
    const _prevActiveLi    = tabBar.querySelector('li.nav-item.active');
    const _prevActivePanel = tabContent.querySelector(':scope > .tab-pane.active, :scope > tab.active');
    if (_prevActiveLi)    R._prevActiveLi    = _prevActiveLi;
    if (_prevActivePanel) R._prevActivePanel = _prevActivePanel;

    // Deactivate all current C7 tabs and panels
    tabBar.querySelectorAll('li.nav-item').forEach(li => {
      li.classList.remove('active');
      const a = li.querySelector('a.nav-link');
      if (a) { a.classList.remove('active'); a.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false'); }
    });
    tabContent.querySelectorAll(':scope > tab, :scope > .tab-pane').forEach(p => {
      p.classList.remove('active');
      p.style.display = 'none';
    });

    // Inject our tab li - close x lives inside the tab label, matching C7/Pack v3 pattern
    const tabLi = document.createElement('li');
    tabLi.id = 'mpk-tab-li';
    tabLi.className = 'nav-item active';
    tabLi.innerHTML = `
      <a class="nav-link active" aria-selected="true" href="javascript:void(0)" style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;padding-right:8px;">
        Malpa Pick
        <span id="mpk-tab-close" title="Close (Esc)" style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:18px;height:18px;border-radius:3px;font-size:14px;line-height:1;color:#384042;cursor:pointer;opacity:.6;margin-left:2px;transition:opacity .15s,background .15s;-webkit-tap-highlight-color:transparent;">x</span>
      </a>`;
    tabBar.appendChild(tabLi);

    // Wire close x - fires on the span only, not the whole tab link
    tabLi.querySelector('#mpk-tab-close').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      closeUI();
    });
    tabLi.querySelector('#mpk-tab-close').addEventListener('mouseenter', (e) => {
      e.target.style.opacity = '1';
      e.target.style.background = 'rgba(0,0,0,.08)';
    });
    tabLi.querySelector('#mpk-tab-close').addEventListener('mouseleave', (e) => {
      e.target.style.opacity = '.6';
      e.target.style.background = '';
    });

    // Inject our panel
    const panel = document.createElement('div');
    panel.id = 'mpk-tab-view';
    panel.className = 'tab-pane active';

    // Build the root structure
    panel.innerHTML = `<div id="mpk-root"></div>`;
    tabContent.appendChild(panel);

    // Attach keyboard listener
    document.addEventListener('keydown', onGlobalKey);

    // Minimise C7 sidebar to give maximum screen space on TC51
    // Store existing state so we can restore exactly on close
    R._sidebarWasMinimized = document.body.classList.contains('sidebar-minimized');
    R._brandWasMinimized   = document.body.classList.contains('brand-minimized');
    document.body.classList.add('sidebar-minimized', 'brand-minimized');

    // Measure exact available height (accounts for Firefox bar, C7 nav, tab bar)
    setTimeout(measureHeight, 50);
    window.addEventListener('resize', measureHeight);

    // Show profile select immediately (with whatever profiles are cached)
    renderProfileSelect();

    // Fetch init data (profiles, container types, reasons) then re-render if needed
    initData().then(() => {
      if (State.screen === 'PROFILE_SELECT') renderProfileSelect();
    });

    // Check for a saved mid-pick resume state
    const _resume = loadPickResumeState();
    if (_resume) {
      // Show resume banner over the profile select
      setTimeout(() => _showResumeBanner(_resume), 400);
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 2: PROFILE SELECT + JOB SUMMARY
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  // -- Init: fetch profiles, container types, reasons in parallel --------------

  async function initData() {
    // Cache guard - skip re-fetch if already loaded (static per session)
    const needsProfiles = State.profiles.length === 0;
    const needsTypes    = State.containerTypes.length === 0;
    const needsReasons  = State.reasons.length === 0;
    if (!needsProfiles && !needsTypes && !needsReasons) {
      console.log('[MalpaPick] initData skipped - already cached');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const fetches = await Promise.all([
        needsProfiles ? fetchProfiles()       : Promise.resolve(State.profiles),
        needsTypes    ? fetchContainerTypes() : Promise.resolve(State.containerTypes),
        needsReasons  ? fetchReasons()        : Promise.resolve(State.reasons),
      ]);
      State.profiles       = fetches[0] || [];
      State.containerTypes = fetches[1] || [];
      State.reasons        = fetches[2] || [];
      console.log('[MalpaPick] initData OK - profiles:', State.profiles.length,
        'containerTypes:', State.containerTypes.length, 'reasons:', State.reasons.length);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[MalpaPick] initData failed:', err.message, err);
      if (State.screen === 'PROFILE_SELECT') {
        renderProfileSelect('Could not load profiles: ' + err.message);
      }
    }
  }

  async function fetchProfiles() {
    // Minimal expand - we only need id, name, initiation_method
    // Removing jobTypes/jobZones/verifications/dynamicInput cuts response size ~70%
    const data = await apiGet(
      'shipment/shipment-picking-profile' +
      '&expand=&per-page=100&page=1'
    );
    return Array.isArray(data) ? data : (data?.items || []);
  }

  async function fetchContainerTypes() {
    const data = await apiGet('configuration/container-type&expand=&per-page=100&page=1');
    return Array.isArray(data) ? data : (data?.items || []);
  }

  async function fetchReasons() {
    const data = await apiGet('configuration/reason&expand=reasonClass&per-page=100&page=1');
    return Array.isArray(data) ? data : (data?.items || []);
  }

  async function fetchJobSummary(profileId) {
    return apiGet(`shipment/shipment-picking-profile/get-job-summary&id=${profileId}`);
  }

  // Fetch all instructions for a job using the standard REST list endpoint.
  // Requires job_id - call after fetchFirstInstruction() has set State.jobId.
  async function fetchJobInstructions(jobId) {
    const EXPAND = encodeURIComponent('item.company,status');
    try {
      const data = await apiGet(
        `job/job-instruction&job_id=${jobId}&per-page=200&page=1&expand=${EXPAND}`
      );
      if (Array.isArray(data)) return data;
      if (data && Array.isArray(data.items)) return data.items;
      return [];
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[MalpaPick] fetchJobInstructions failed:', e.message);
      return [];
    }
  }

  async function fetchFirstInstruction(profileId, jobNum) {
    const EXPAND = [
      'fromLocation', 'toLocation',
      'item.itemUnitOfMeasures.itemUnitOfMeasureReference',
      'item.itemUnitOfMeasures.unitOfMeasure',
      'batch', 'license_plate_no', 'shipmentNumber',
      'itemUnitOfMeasure.unitOfMeasure',
      'jobInstructionGroup.id',
      'shipmentDetailChildren', 'item.company', 'custom_field_1',
    ].join(',');
    let path = `shipment/shipment-picking-profile/get-job-instructions` +
      `&id=${profileId}&expand=${encodeURIComponent(EXPAND)}`;
    if (jobNum) {
      path += `&job_num=${encodeURIComponent(jobNum)}`;
    }
    const data = await apiGet(path);
    const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
    if (!arr.length) return null;
    const instr = arr[0];
    State.instruction = instr;
    State.jobId       = instr.job_id || null;
    return instr;
  }

  // -- Screen A: Profile select ------------------------------------------------

  function renderProfileSelect(errorMsg) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;
    R.root = root;
    setTimeout(measureHeight, 30);

    const profileOptions = State.profiles.length
      ? '<option value="" disabled selected>-- Select profile --</option>' +
        State.profiles.map(p =>
          `<option value="${p.id}">${_esc(p.name)}</option>`
        ).join('')
      : '<option value="" disabled>No profiles available</option>';

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-screen">
        <div class="mpk-screen-header">Malpa Pick</div>
        <div class="mpk-screen-body">
          ${errorMsg ? `<div class="mpk-error-banner">${_esc(errorMsg)}</div>` : ''}
          <label style="font-size:13px;color:#384042;font-weight:500;margin-bottom:2px;">
            Select Picking Profile
          </label>
          <select id="mpk-profile-sel" class="mpk-select">
            ${profileOptions}
          </select>
          ${State.profiles.length === 0
            ? '<div class="mpk-empty-queue"><div class="mpk-empty-queue-title">No profiles loaded</div><div class="mpk-empty-queue-sub">Check your connection and try again</div></div>'
            : ''}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-spacer"></div>
      <div class="mpk-btn-stack">
        <button id="mpk-start-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-primary" ${State.profiles.length === 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>
          Start Picking
        </button>
      </div>`;

    R.profileSel = document.getElementById('mpk-profile-sel');
    R.startBtn   = document.getElementById('mpk-start-btn');

    if (R.startBtn) {
      R.startBtn.addEventListener('click', onStartPicking);
    }

    // Pre-select previously chosen profile
    if (R.profileSel && State.profile) {
      R.profileSel.value = String(State.profile.id);
    }

    State.screen = 'PROFILE_SELECT';
  }

  async function onStartPicking() {
    if (!R.profileSel) return;
    const profileId = parseInt(R.profileSel.value, 10);
    if (!profileId || isNaN(profileId)) return;

    const profile = State.profiles.find(p => p.id === profileId) || null;
    State.profile = profile;

    // initiation_method=2: Wholesale Queue, Supervisor Bypass, Wholesale - Pick Consign
    // These require a shipment number - show the job_num entry screen instead
    if (profile && profile.initiation_method === 2) {
      renderJobNumEntry(profile);
      return;
    }

    // initiation_method=1: queue-based - fetch next job automatically
    if (R.startBtn) {
      R.startBtn.disabled = true;
      R.startBtn.textContent = 'Loading?';
    }

    try {
      const instruction = await fetchFirstInstruction(profileId);
      if (!instruction) {
        renderNoJobs(profile);
        return;
      }
      const summary = { total_instructions: '?', total_jobs: 1, total_weight: null };
      State.summary = summary;
      renderJobSummary(summary, instruction, profile);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[MalpaPick] onStartPicking error:', err.message);
      renderProfileSelect('Failed to load job: ' + err.message);
    }
  }

  // -- Job number entry screen (initiation_method=2 profiles) -----------------

  function renderJobNumEntry(profile, errorMsg) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-screen">
        <div class="mpk-screen-header">Enter Shipment Number</div>
        <div class="mpk-screen-body">
          <div class="mpk-profile-badge">
            <span class="mpk-profile-badge-dot"></span>
            ${_esc(profile.name)}
          </div>
          ${errorMsg ? `<div class="mpk-error-banner">${_esc(errorMsg)}</div>` : ''}
          <label style="font-size:13px;color:#384042;font-weight:500;margin-bottom:2px;">
            Shipment Number
          </label>
          <input
            id="mpk-jobnum-in"
            class="mpk-input"
            type="text"
            inputmode="none"
            autocomplete="off"
            autocorrect="off"
            autocapitalize="off"
            placeholder="Scan or type shipment number"
            value="${_esc(State._lastJobNum || '')}"
          />
          <div class="mpk-jobnum-hint">
            Scan the shipment barcode or type the number manually
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-spacer"></div>
      <div class="mpk-btn-stack">
        <button id="mpk-load-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-primary">Load Job</button>
        <button id="mpk-back-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">&lt;- Back</button>
      </div>`;

    const jobNumIn = document.getElementById('mpk-jobnum-in');
    const loadBtn  = document.getElementById('mpk-load-btn');
    const backBtn  = document.getElementById('mpk-back-btn');

    // Allow scanner to fill the input then auto-submit on Enter
    jobNumIn?.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter' && jobNumIn.value.trim()) {
        e.preventDefault();
        onLoadJobNum(profile, jobNumIn.value.trim());
      }
    });

    loadBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const val = jobNumIn?.value.trim();
      if (val) onLoadJobNum(profile, val);
    });

    backBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => renderProfileSelect());

    // Auto-focus for scanner
    setTimeout(() => jobNumIn?.focus(), 80);
    State.screen = 'JOB_NUM_ENTRY';
  }

  async function onLoadJobNum(profile, jobNum) {
    State._lastJobNum = jobNum;
    const loadBtn = document.getElementById('mpk-load-btn');
    if (loadBtn) { loadBtn.disabled = true; loadBtn.textContent = 'Loading?'; }

    try {
      const instruction = await fetchFirstInstruction(profile.id, jobNum);

      if (!instruction) {
        renderJobNumEntry(profile, `No job found for shipment: ${jobNum}`);
        return;
      }

      const summary = { total_instructions: '?', total_jobs: 1, total_weight: null };
      State.summary = summary;
      renderJobSummary(summary, instruction, profile);

    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[MalpaPick] onLoadJobNum error:', err.message);
      renderJobNumEntry(profile, 'Failed to load job: ' + err.message);
    }
  }

  // -- No jobs state -----------------------------------------------------------

  function renderNoJobs(profile) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-screen">
        <div class="mpk-screen-header">Malpa Pick</div>
        <div class="mpk-screen-body">
          <div class="mpk-empty-queue">
            <div class="mpk-empty-queue-icon" style="font-size:28px;font-weight:700;color:#9faecb">[0]</div>
            <div class="mpk-empty-queue-title">No jobs in queue</div>
            <div class="mpk-empty-queue-sub">
              ${_esc(profile ? profile.name : 'This profile')} has no pending jobs
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-spacer"></div>
      <div class="mpk-btn-stack">
        <button id="mpk-back-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">&lt;- Back</button>
      </div>`;

    document.getElementById('mpk-back-btn')
      ?.addEventListener('click', () => renderProfileSelect());
    State.screen = 'NO_JOBS';
  }

  // -- Screen B: Job summary ---------------------------------------------------

  // Profile colour map - keyed by profile ID
  // Fallback: method=2 (manual) = blue, method=1 clusters = teal family, SIBP/MIBP = amber
  function profileColour(profile) {
    const MAP = {
      40: '#00897b', // Group 1 - teal
      42: '#00acc1', // Group 2 - cyan
      43: '#039be5', // Group 3 - light blue
      44: '#3949ab', // Group 4 - indigo
      45: '#8e24aa', // Group 5 - purple
      46: '#d81b60', // Group 6 - pink
      47: '#f9a825', // SIBP - yellow ?
      48: '#fb8c00', // MIBP - orange
      49: '#1e88e5', // Wholesale Queue - blue
      50: '#e53935', // Supervisor Bypass - red
      51: '#00838f', // WavePicker Clusters - dark cyan
      52: '#6d4c41', // Bulky Cluster - brown
      53: '#1565c0', // Wholesale Cluster - dark blue
      54: '#558b2f', // LOCOD - green
      55: '#6a1b9a', // Wine - deep purple
      56: '#00695c', // WavePicker SIBP - dark teal
      57: '#e65100', // MIBP Liquid - deep orange
      58: '#c62828', // Priority Cluster - deep red
      59: '#1976d2', // Wholesale Pick Consign - blue
    };
    return MAP[profile?.id] || '#20a8d8';
  }

  function renderJobSummary(summary, instruction, profile) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;

    const profileName = profile?.name || '-';
    const colour      = profileColour(profile);
    const startingLocation = instruction?.fromLocation?.location_code || '-';
    const SPIN        = '<span class="mpk-spinner" style="width:14px;height:14px;border-width:2px;display:inline-block"></span>';

    // Render immediately - counts show spinners until background fetch completes
    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-screen">
        <div class="mpk-screen-header">Job Summary</div>
        <div class="mpk-screen-body">
          <div class="mpk-summary-card" style="--mpk-profile-color:${colour}">
            <div class="mpk-summary-profile">
              <span class="mpk-summary-profile-dot"></span>
              ${_esc(profileName)}
            </div>
            <div class="mpk-summary-rows">
              <div class="mpk-summary-row">
                <span class="mpk-summary-label">Starting location</span>
                <span class="mpk-summary-value hi">${_esc(startingLocation)}</span>
              </div>
              <div class="mpk-summary-row">
                <span class="mpk-summary-label">Job type</span>
                <span class="mpk-summary-value">${_esc(profileName)}</span>
              </div>
              <div class="mpk-summary-row">
                <span class="mpk-summary-label">Shipments</span>
                <span class="mpk-summary-value" id="mpk-sum-shipments">${SPIN}</span>
              </div>
              <div class="mpk-summary-row">
                <span class="mpk-summary-label">Instructions</span>
                <span class="mpk-summary-value" id="mpk-sum-instructions">${SPIN}</span>
              </div>
              <div class="mpk-summary-row">
                <span class="mpk-summary-label">Total quantity</span>
                <span class="mpk-summary-value" id="mpk-sum-qty">${SPIN}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-spacer"></div>
      <div class="mpk-btn-stack">
        <button id="mpk-accept-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-primary">Accept Job</button>
        <button id="mpk-back-btn"   class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">&lt;- Back</button>
      </div>`;

    R.acceptBtn = document.getElementById('mpk-accept-btn');
    R.backBtn   = document.getElementById('mpk-back-btn');
    R.acceptBtn?.addEventListener('click', onAcceptJob);
    R.backBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      unassignJob(State.jobId);
      State.jobId = null;
      State.instruction = null;
      State.allInstructions = [];
      renderProfileSelect();
    });
    State.screen = 'JOB_SUMMARY';

    // Fetch counts in background - update cells in-place when ready
    if (State.jobId) {
      fetchJobInstructions(State.jobId).then(all => {
        const upd = (id, val) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = val; };
        if (!document.getElementById('mpk-sum-shipments')) return; // navigated away
        if (all.length) {
          State.allInstructions = all; // cache for Fragment 4 pick loop
          upd('mpk-sum-shipments', new Set(all.map(i => i.reference_number).filter(Boolean)).size);
          upd('mpk-sum-qty',       all.reduce((s, i) => s + (i.quantity || 0), 0));
          // Deduplicate by group_id - each group = 1 pick action
          const seenGroups = new Set();
          let pickTotal = 0;
          for (const i of all) {
            if (i.job_instruction_group_id) {
              if (!seenGroups.has(i.job_instruction_group_id)) {
                seenGroups.add(i.job_instruction_group_id);
                pickTotal++;
              }
            } else {
              pickTotal++;
            }
          }
          // Show deduplicated count on summary (matches progress bar)
          upd('mpk-sum-instructions', pickTotal);
          // Set or update pickProgress -- may already exist if Accept Job fired first
          if (!State.pickProgress || State.pickProgress.total === '?') {
            State.pickProgress = { current: State.pickProgress?.current || 1, total: pickTotal };
          } else {
            State.pickProgress.total = pickTotal; // correct the total with deduped count
          }
          // Update progress bar if pick screen is already showing
          if (State.screen === 'PICK_ITEM' || State.screen === 'SCAN_CONTAINER') {
            const txt = document.querySelector('.mpk-loc-progress-text');
            if (txt) txt.textContent = (State.pickProgress.current) + ' / ' + pickTotal + ' instructions';
            const fill = document.querySelector('.mpk-progress-fill');
            if (fill) fill.style.width = Math.round(((State.pickProgress.current-1)/pickTotal)*100) + '%';
          }
        } else {
          ['mpk-sum-shipments','mpk-sum-instructions','mpk-sum-qty'].forEach(id => upd(id, '-'));
        }
      }).catch(() => {
        ['mpk-sum-shipments','mpk-sum-instructions','mpk-sum-qty'].forEach(id => {
          const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '-';
        });
      });
    }
  }

  async function onAcceptJob() {
    State.screen = 'PICKING';
    Audio.init();

    // Build barcode->instruction lookup from cached allInstructions
    State.barcodeMap = {};
    for (const instr of State.allInstructions) {
      const refs = instr.item?.itemUnitOfMeasures?.flatMap(
        u => u.itemUnitOfMeasureReference?.map(r => r.reference?.toLowerCase()) || []
      ) || [];
      if (instr.item?.item_code) refs.push(instr.item.item_code.toLowerCase());
      for (const ref of refs) {
        if (ref) State.barcodeMap[ref] = instr;
      }
    }

    // Set progress total -- use allInstructions if available,
    // fall back to summary.total_instructions, then update when allInstrs resolves
    if (!State.pickProgress) {
      const total = State.allInstructions.length > 0
        ? (() => {
            const seen = new Set();
            let n = 0;
            for (const i of State.allInstructions) {
              if (i.job_instruction_group_id) {
                if (!seen.has(i.job_instruction_group_id)) { seen.add(i.job_instruction_group_id); n++; }
              } else { n++; }
            }
            return n;
          })()
        : (typeof State.summary?.total_instructions === 'number'
            ? State.summary.total_instructions
            : null);
      State.pickProgress = { current: 1, total: total || '?' };
    }

    // Build container prefix list for fast O(1) validation
    State.containerPrefixes = State.containerTypes
      .map(ct => (ct.container_number_prefix || '').toUpperCase())
      .filter(Boolean);

    // If first instruction is grouped, fetch group record before showing pick screen
    await loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(State.instruction);
    renderPickScreen(State.instruction);
  }

  // -- Utility -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function _esc(str) {
    return String(str ?? '').replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({
      '&': '&amp;', '<': '&lt;', '>': '&gt;', '"': '&quot;', "'": '&#39;',
    }[c]));
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 3: PICK SCREEN + VOICE + AUDIO
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  // -- Voice engine -------------------------------------------------------------

  // Format a location code for natural speech
  // e.g. "A11-B08-S11" -> "A 11, B 8, S 11"
  //      "01"           -> "1"
  //      "B19"          -> "B 19"
  // prevLoc: if same leading segment (e.g. same A aisle), skip it
  // e.g. prev="A12-B24-S12", loc="A12-B26-S11" -> "B 26, S 11"
  function _formatLocForSpeech(loc, prevLoc) {
    if (!loc) return '';
    const segs     = loc.split('-');
    const prevSegs = prevLoc ? prevLoc.split('-') : [];
    // Skip matching leading segments (but always say at least the last one)
    let skipCount = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < segs.length - 1; i++) {
      if (prevSegs[i] && prevSegs[i].toUpperCase() === segs[i].toUpperCase()) {
        skipCount++;
      } else {
        break;
      }
    }
    return segs.slice(skipCount).map(seg => {
      const m = seg.match(/^([A-Za-z]*)(\d+)$/);
      if (!m) return seg;
      const letters = m[1];
      const num     = parseInt(m[2], 10);
      if (!letters) return String(num);
      return letters + ' ' + num;
    }).join(', ');
  }

  const Voice = {
    speak(text) {
      if (!State.voiceEnabled) return;
      if (!window.speechSynthesis) return;
      window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
      const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(String(text));
      utt.rate  = 1.8;
      utt.pitch = 1.0;
      utt.volume = 1.0;
      window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    },

    announceInstruction(instruction, prevInstruction) {
      if (!instruction) return;
      const loc     = instruction.fromLocation?.location_code || '';
      const qty     = displayQty(instruction);
      const desc    = instruction.item?.abc_category || instruction.item?.description || '';
      const uom     = instruction.itemUnitOfMeasure?.unitOfMeasure?.name || '';
      let uomStr = '';
      if (uom && uom.toLowerCase() !== 'each') {
        const plural = qty > 1 && !uom.toLowerCase().endsWith('s') ? uom + 's' : uom;
        uomStr = ` ${plural}`;
      }
      const prevLoc = prevInstruction?.fromLocation?.location_code || '';
      const locSpoken = _formatLocForSpeech(loc, prevLoc);
      // Just location, quantity and item -- no filler words
      this.speak(`Go to ${locSpoken}. Pick ${qty}${uomStr} ${desc}`);
    },

    announcePosition(positionId) {
      this.speak(`Position ${positionId}`);
    },

    cancel() {
      if (window.speechSynthesis) window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
    },

    // Speak an error -- bypasses voiceEnabled toggle (always active)
    error(msg) {
      if (!window.speechSynthesis) return;
      window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
      const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(String(msg));
      utt.rate   = 1.7;
      utt.pitch  = 1.0;
      utt.volume = 1.0;
      window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    },
  };

  // -- Audio engine -------------------------------------------------------------
  const Audio = {
    _ctx: null,

    init() {
      if (this._ctx) return;
      try {
        this._ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('[MalpaPick] AudioContext unavailable:', e.message);
      }
    },

    _tone(freq, duration, type = 'sine', gainVal = 0.4, startDelay = 0) {
      if (!this._ctx) return;
      try {
        const osc  = this._ctx.createOscillator();
        const gain = this._ctx.createGain();
        osc.connect(gain);
        gain.connect(this._ctx.destination);
        osc.type = type;
        osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, this._ctx.currentTime + startDelay);
        gain.gain.setValueAtTime(gainVal, this._ctx.currentTime + startDelay);
        gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, this._ctx.currentTime + startDelay + duration);
        osc.start(this._ctx.currentTime + startDelay);
        osc.stop(this._ctx.currentTime + startDelay + duration);
      } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
    },

    _playMp3(b64DataUri) {
      if (!b64DataUri) return;
      try {
        const a = new window.Audio(b64DataUri);
        a.volume = 1.0;
        a.play().catch(() => {});
      } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
    },

    chime(type) {
      this.init();

      if (type === 'item_done') {
        if (!this._ctx) return;
        if (this._ctx.state === 'suspended') this._ctx.resume();
        // Single clean high ping - item quantity verified
        this._tone(880, 0.15, 'sine', 0.35, 0);
        this._tone(880, 0.10, 'sine', 0.15, 0.15);

      } else if (type === 'container_ok') {
        if (!this._ctx) return;
        if (this._ctx.state === 'suspended') this._ctx.resume();
        // Two-note ascending rise - container accepted, moving on
        this._tone(660, 0.12, 'sine', 0.3, 0);
        this._tone(880, 0.20, 'sine', 0.4, 0.13);

      } else if (type === 'error') {
        // Short double-buzz - noticeable but not obnoxious
        if (!this._ctx) return;
        if (this._ctx.state === 'suspended') this._ctx.resume();
        this._tone(180, 0.08, 'square', 0.3, 0.00);
        this._tone(180, 0.08, 'square', 0.3, 0.12);

      } else if (type === 'error_donkey') {
        // Donkey sound - reserved for short-pick (Fragment 8)
        if (_DONKEY_B64) {
          this._playMp3(_DONKEY_B64);
        } else {
          if (!this._ctx) return;
          if (this._ctx.state === 'suspended') this._ctx.resume();
          this._tone(200, 0.3, 'sawtooth', 0.3, 0);
        }
      }
    },
  };

  // -- Progress (lives inside the blue location header) ------------------------
  function updateProgressBar(current, total) {
    const fill = document.querySelector('.mpk-progress-fill');
    const text = document.querySelector('.mpk-loc-progress-text');
    if (!fill || !text) return;
    const pct = (total > 0) ? Math.round((current / total) * 100) : 0;
    fill.style.width = pct + '%';
    text.textContent = `${current} / ${total}`;
  }

  // -- Pick screen ---------------------------------------------------------------
  function renderPickScreen(instruction) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;
    State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';

    const loc        = instruction?.fromLocation?.location_code || '-';
    const checkDig   = instruction?.fromLocation?.check_digit   || '';
    const sku        = instruction?.item?.item_code             || '-';
    const desc       = instruction?.item?.abc_category || instruction?.item?.description || '';
    const qty        = displayQty(instruction);   // display qty (raw / factor)
    const shipNum    = instruction?.reference_number || '';
    const uomName    = instruction?.itemUnitOfMeasure?.unitOfMeasure?.name || '';
    const showUom    = uomName && uomName.toLowerCase() !== 'each';
    const clusterPos = instruction?.cluster_position_id;
    const container  = clusterPos ? (State.containersByPosition[clusterPos] || '') : '';

    const progCurrent = State.pickProgress?.current || 1;
    const progTotal   = State.pickProgress?.total   || '?';
    const pct         = progTotal !== '?' ? Math.round(((progCurrent - 1) / progTotal) * 100) : 0;

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-pick-screen" id="mpk-pick-screen">
        <div class="mpk-loc-header">
          <div class="mpk-loc-header-top">
            <span class="mpk-loc-label">Location</span>
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px">
              <span class="mpk-loc-progress-text">${progCurrent} / ${progTotal} instructions</span>
              <button class="mpk-voice-toggle${State.voiceEnabled ? '' : ' muted'}" id="mpk-voice-btn" title="Toggle voice" aria-label="Toggle voice">${State.voiceEnabled ? '\uD83D\uDD0A' : '\uD83D\uDD07'}</button>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-loc-code">${_esc(loc)}</div>
          ${shipNum ? `<div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);font-weight:500;margin-top:2px;letter-spacing:.02em">Shipment: ${_esc(shipNum)}</div>` : ''}
          <div class="mpk-progress-track">
            <div class="mpk-progress-fill" style="width:${pct}%"></div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-item-block">
          <div class="mpk-qty-label">Pick</div>
          <div class="mpk-qty-value">${qty}</div>
          ${showUom ? `<div class="mpk-qty-uom">${_esc(uomName)}</div>` : ''}
          <div class="mpk-item-sku">${_esc(sku)}</div>
          <div class="mpk-item-desc">${_esc(desc)}</div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-scan-area">
          <div class="mpk-scan-zone" id="mpk-scan-zone">
            <div class="mpk-scan-zone-label">Scan item</div>
            <div class="mpk-scan-arrows">&gt;&gt;&gt;</div>
            <input
              id="mpk-scan-in"
              type="text"
              inputmode="none"
              autocomplete="off"
              autocorrect="off"
              autocapitalize="off"
              spellcheck="false"
            />
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-scan-feedback dim" id="mpk-scan-fb">Ready to scan</div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-cluster-strip${clusterPos ? ' visible' : ''}" id="mpk-cluster-strip">
          <span class="mpk-cluster-pos-badge">${clusterPos ?? ''}</span>
          <span class="mpk-cluster-pos-label">Position ${clusterPos ?? ''}</span>
          <span class="mpk-cluster-container${container ? ' assigned' : ''}" id="mpk-cluster-container">${container ? _esc(container) : 'No tote yet'}</span>
        </div>

      </div>
      <div class="mpk-pick-actions">
        <button id="mpk-shortpick-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">Short Pick</button>
      </div>`;

    R.scanIn       = document.getElementById('mpk-scan-in');
    R.scanFb       = document.getElementById('mpk-scan-fb');
    R.shortPickBtn = document.getElementById('mpk-shortpick-btn');

    if (R.scanIn) {
      R.scanIn.addEventListener('keydown', _onScanKeydown);
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 80);
    }

    R.shortPickBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => showShortPickFlow(State.instruction));


    document.getElementById('mpk-voice-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      State.voiceEnabled = !State.voiceEnabled;
      try { sessionStorage.setItem('mpk_voice', State.voiceEnabled ? '1' : '0'); } catch(_) {}
      const btn = document.getElementById('mpk-voice-btn');
      if (btn) {
        btn.textContent  = State.voiceEnabled ? '\uD83D\uDD0A' : '\uD83D\uDD07';
        btn.classList.toggle('muted', !State.voiceEnabled);
        btn.title = State.voiceEnabled ? 'Voice on' : 'Voice off';
      }
      if (!State.voiceEnabled) Voice.cancel();
      // Re-focus scan input so scanner works immediately after toggling
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 80);
    });

    // Refocus scan input on any tap anywhere in the pick screen
    document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen')?.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      if (e.target.closest('button')) return;
      // Route to correct input based on active screen
      const inputId = State.screen === 'SHORT_PICK_LOCATION' ? 'mpk-sp-scan-in' : 'mpk-scan-in';
      setTimeout(() => document.getElementById(inputId)?.focus(), 50);
    });

    setTimeout(measureHeight, 30);
    // Delay ensures no cancellation from DOM operations happening right after
    setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(instruction), 150);
  }

  // Scan keydown handler - Fragment 4 will replace _onScan with full logic
  function _onScanKeydown(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.keyCode === 13) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const val = R.scanIn?.value?.trim();
      if (val) {
        _onScan(val);
        if (R.scanIn) R.scanIn.value = '';
      }
    }
  }

  // _onScan - master scan router
  function _onScan(barcode) {
    const s = State.screen;
    if (s === 'TRANSITIONING') return; // ignore scans during screen transitions
    if (s === 'PICK_ITEM')           onItemScan(barcode);
    else if (s === 'SCAN_CONTAINER') onContainerScan(barcode);
    else if (s === 'QTY_MODAL')      onQtyModalScan(barcode);
  }

  function setScanFeedback(msg, type) {
    if (!R.scanFb) return;
    R.scanFb.textContent = msg;
    R.scanFb.className = 'mpk-scan-feedback ' + (type || 'dim');

    // Full-screen colour flash - faster to process than text in high-intensity env
    if (type === 'ok' || type === 'err') {
      const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
      if (screen) {
        const flash = document.createElement('div');
        flash.className = 'mpk-flash ' + (type === 'ok' ? 'flash-ok' : 'flash-err');
        screen.style.position = 'relative';
        screen.appendChild(flash);
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
          flash.style.opacity = '0.35';
          setTimeout(() => {
            flash.style.opacity = '0';
            setTimeout(() => flash.remove(), 80);
          }, 80);
        });
      }
      // Tactile vibration - adds channel for noisy/eyes-busy situations
      if (navigator.vibrate) {
        navigator.vibrate(type === 'ok' ? [30] : [60, 30, 60]);
      }
    }
  }


  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 8: SHORT PICK FLOW
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  // -- pick-short API call ----------------------------------------------------
  async function performShortPick(instruction, reasonCode, partialQty, containerNo) {
    // correlation_id matches C7's own format: sp_{timestamp}_{random}
    const correlationId = `sp_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,15)}`;
    return apiPost(
      `job/job-instruction/pick-short&id=${instruction.id}`,
      {
        container_no:         containerNo || '',
        quantity:             0,
        quantity_entry_mode:  'units',
        container_type_id:    null,
        profile_id:           null,
        is_tracking:          null,
        ship_no:              instruction.reference_number,
        from_location:        instruction.from_location_id,
        item_id:              instruction.item_id,
        picking_qty:          instruction.quantity,
        reason_code:          reasonCode || '',
        correlation_id:       correlationId,
      }
    );
  }

  // -- Step 1: Check digit scan -----------------------------------------------
  function showShortPickFlow(instruction) {
    const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
    if (!screen) return;

    // Remove any existing overlay
    document.getElementById('mpk-sp-overlay')?.remove();

    const loc      = instruction?.fromLocation?.location_code || '-';
    // We store check_digit for validation but NEVER display it to the picker
    const expected = instruction?.fromLocation?.check_digit || '';

    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'mpk-sp-overlay';
    overlay.id = 'mpk-sp-overlay';
    overlay.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-sp-header">
        <span class="mpk-sp-title">Short Pick</span>
        <button class="mpk-sp-close" id="mpk-sp-close">x</button>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-sp-body">
        <div class="mpk-sp-loc">${_esc(loc)}</div>
        <div class="mpk-sp-instruction">
          Scan the location check digit to confirm<br>you are at the correct shelf
        </div>
        <div class="mpk-sp-scan-zone">
          <div class="mpk-sp-scan-label">Scan check digit</div>
          <div class="mpk-sp-arrows">&gt;&gt;&gt;</div>
          <input id="mpk-sp-scan-in" type="text" inputmode="none"
            autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off"
            spellcheck="false"
            style="position:absolute;width:1px;height:1px;opacity:0;top:0;left:0"/>
        </div>
        <div class="mpk-sp-feedback dim" id="mpk-sp-fb">Ready to scan</div>
      </div>`;

    screen.appendChild(overlay);
    State.screen = 'SHORT_PICK_LOCATION';

    const spInput = document.getElementById('mpk-sp-scan-in');
    const spFb    = document.getElementById('mpk-sp-fb');

    // Ensure input can receive events -- move out of scan zone to overlay root
    // so position:absolute sits within the full overlay, not clipped by zone
    if (spInput) {
      overlay.appendChild(spInput);
    }

    document.getElementById('mpk-sp-close')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      overlay.remove();
      State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 80);
    });

    spInput?.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key !== 'Enter' && e.keyCode !== 13) return;
      e.preventDefault();
      const val = spInput.value.trim();
      spInput.value = '';
      if (!val) return;

      if (!expected) {
        // No check digit configured - skip directly to reason select
        overlay.remove();
        showShortPickReason(instruction);
        return;
      }

      if (val.toLowerCase() === String(expected).toLowerCase()) {
        // Correct - advance to reason selection
        overlay.remove();
        showShortPickReason(instruction);
      } else {
        // Wrong location
        Audio.chime('error');
        if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([60, 30, 60]);
        Voice.error('Wrong check digit');
        spFb.textContent = 'Wrong location - try again';
        spFb.className = 'mpk-sp-feedback err';
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (spFb) { spFb.textContent = 'Scan the location barcode'; spFb.className = 'mpk-sp-feedback dim'; }
          spInput?.focus(); // re-focus after error
        }, 2000);
      }
    });

    setTimeout(() => { spInput?.focus(); }, 200);
  }

  // -- Step 2: Reason select --------------------------------------------------
  function showShortPickReason(instruction) {
    const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
    if (!screen) return;

    // Filter to short_pick_class (class_id = 5) from cached reasons
    const shortPickReasons = State.reasons.filter(r => r.reason_class_id === 5);

    // Reason icons
    const ICONS = { 'Out Of Reach': '?', 'Stock Not Present': '?', 'Damaged': '?' };

    const reasonBtns = shortPickReasons.length
      ? shortPickReasons.map(r =>
          `<button class="mpk-reason-btn" data-rid="${r.id}" data-rcode="${_esc(r.reason_code)}">
            <span class="mpk-reason-icon">${ICONS[r.reason_code] || '[!]'}</span>
            ${_esc(r.reason_code)}
           </button>`
        ).join('')
      : '<div style="color:#9faecb;font-size:13px">No reason codes available</div>';

    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'mpk-sp-overlay';
    overlay.id = 'mpk-sp-overlay';
    overlay.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-sp-header">
        <span class="mpk-sp-title">Short Pick - Select Reason</span>
        <button class="mpk-sp-close" id="mpk-sp-close">x</button>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-sp-body">
        <div class="mpk-sp-instruction" style="margin-bottom:4px">
          Why can't you pick the full quantity?
        </div>
        <div class="mpk-reason-list">${reasonBtns}</div>
      </div>`;

    screen.appendChild(overlay);
    State.screen = 'SHORT_PICK_REASON';

    document.getElementById('mpk-sp-close')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      overlay.remove();
      State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 80);
    });

    overlay.querySelectorAll('.mpk-reason-btn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const reasonCode = btn.dataset.rcode || '';
        overlay.remove();
        onShortPickConfirm(instruction, reasonCode);
      });
    });
  }

  // -- Step 3: Submit short pick ----------------------------------------------
  async function onShortPickConfirm(instruction, reasonCode) {
    const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
    if (!screen) return;

    // Show confirming state
    State.screen = 'TRANSITIONING';
    setScanFeedback('Confirming short pick?', 'dim');

    // Short pick: nothing was picked so nothing goes into any tote
    // Always send empty container_no regardless of cluster position assignment
    const containerNo = '';

    try {
      const result = await performShortPick(instruction, reasonCode, 0, containerNo);

      Audio.chime('container_ok');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([30]);

      // Advance progress
      if (State.pickProgress) State.pickProgress.current++;

      // change-sequence fires after short pick (matches C7 behaviour)
      changeSequence(instruction.id);

      const isJobDone = result.job_instruction === null;

      if (isJobDone) {
        renderJobComplete(false);
      } else {
        const fullNext = await fetchNextInstruction(result.job_instruction);
        const nextInstr = fullNext || result.job_instruction;
        State.instruction = nextInstr;
        State.jobId = nextInstr.job_id || State.jobId;
        await loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(nextInstr);
        renderPickScreen(nextInstr);
        setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(nextInstr), 150);
      }

    } catch (err) {
      State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';
      setScanFeedback(err.message || 'Short pick failed - try again', 'err');
      Audio.chime('error');
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 100);
    }
  }

  function _showNotImpl(label) {
    setScanFeedback(label, 'dim');
  }

  // -- Resume banner (shown on re-open when mid-pick state exists) -----------
  function _showResumeBanner(resumeState) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;

    // Find the matching profile
    const profile = State.profiles.find(p => p.id === resumeState.profileId);
    const profileName = profile?.name || `Profile ${resumeState.profileId}`;

    const banner = document.createElement('div');
    banner.id = 'mpk-resume-banner';
    banner.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute;inset:0;z-index:500;background:rgba(0,0,0,.7)',
      'display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center',
      'padding:24px;gap:14px;text-align:center',
    ].join(';');
    banner.innerHTML = `
      <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:#fff">RESUME</div>
      <div style="font-size:17px;font-weight:700;color:#fff">Resume picking?</div>
      <div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);line-height:1.5">
        You have an active pick job for<br>
        <strong style="color:#fabb3d">${_esc(profileName)}</strong><br>
        <span style="font-size:11px;opacity:.7">
          Pick ${resumeState.pickProgressCurrent} of ${resumeState.pickProgressTotal}
        </span>
      </div>
      <button id="mpk-resume-yes" style="
        width:100%;padding:14px;background:#20a8d8;color:#fff;border:none;
        font-size:15px;font-weight:600;font-family:Roboto,sans-serif;
        cursor:pointer;border-radius:4px;
      ">Resume Pick</button>
      <button id="mpk-resume-no" style="
        width:100%;padding:12px;background:transparent;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);
        border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.2);font-size:13px;font-weight:500;
        font-family:Roboto,sans-serif;cursor:pointer;border-radius:4px;
      ">Start Fresh</button>`;

    root.style.position = 'relative';
    root.appendChild(banner);

    document.getElementById('mpk-resume-yes')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      banner.remove();
      await _resumePickFromState(resumeState);
    });

    document.getElementById('mpk-resume-no')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      clearPickResumeState();
      banner.remove();
    });
  }

  async function _resumePickFromState(resumeState) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;

    // Show loading
    root.innerHTML = `<div class="mpk-loading"><div class="mpk-spinner"></div>Resuming pick?</div>`;

    try {
      // Restore profile
      const profile = State.profiles.find(p => p.id === resumeState.profileId);
      if (!profile) throw new Error('Profile not found');
      State.profile = profile;
      State.jobId   = resumeState.jobId;

      // Restore container positions
      State.containersByPosition = resumeState.containersByPosition || {};

      // Build prefix list
      State.containerPrefixes = State.containerTypes
        .map(ct => (ct.container_number_prefix || '').toUpperCase())
        .filter(Boolean);

      // Fetch the current instruction fresh from API
      const instruction = await fetchFirstInstruction(profile.id);
      if (!instruction) {
        // Job may have completed while away
        clearPickResumeState();
        renderProfileSelect('Job is no longer available - it may have been completed.');
        return;
      }

      State.instruction = instruction;
      State.jobId       = instruction.job_id || resumeState.jobId;

      // Rebuild barcodeMap
      if (!State.allInstructions.length) {
        State.allInstructions = await fetchJobInstructions(State.jobId).catch(() => []);
      }
      State.barcodeMap = {};
      for (const instr of State.allInstructions) {
        const refs = instr.item?.itemUnitOfMeasures?.flatMap(
          u => u.itemUnitOfMeasureReference?.map(r => r.reference?.toLowerCase()) || []
        ) || [];
        if (instr.item?.item_code) refs.push(instr.item.item_code.toLowerCase());
        for (const ref of refs) { if (ref) State.barcodeMap[ref] = instr; }
      }

      // Restore progress
      State.pickProgress = {
        current: resumeState.pickProgressCurrent,
        total:   resumeState.pickProgressTotal,
      };

      Audio.init();
      await loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(instruction);
      renderPickScreen(instruction);

    } catch(err) {
      console.error('[MalpaPick] resume failed:', err.message);
      clearPickResumeState();
      renderProfileSelect('Could not resume - starting fresh. (' + err.message + ')');
    }
  }


  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 5: GROUPED PICK LOOP (SIBP / MIBP)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  // Fetch group record for a grouped instruction - stores in State.groupRecord
  async function loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(instruction) {
    const groupId = instruction?.job_instruction_group_id;
    if (!groupId) {
      State.groupRecord = null;
      return;
    }
    try {
      const EXPAND = encodeURIComponent(
        'fromLocation,toLocation,item.itemUnitOfMeasures.unitOfMeasure,' +
        'item.itemUnitOfMeasures.itemUnitOfMeasureReference,batch,license_plate_no,' +
        'shipmentNumber,itemUnitOfMeasure.unitOfMeasure,jobInstructionGroup.id'
      );
      const data = await apiGet(
        `shipment/shipment-picking-profile/get-job-instruction-groups&id=${groupId}&expand=${EXPAND}`
      );
      const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
      State.groupRecord = arr[0] || null;
      console.log('[MalpaPick] groupRecord loaded:', State.groupRecord);
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[MalpaPick] loadGroupRecordIfNeeded failed:', e.message);
      State.groupRecord = null;
    }
  }

  // Effective quantity to show and pick:
  // - Grouped instruction: groupRecord.units (total across all shipments)
  // - Standard instruction: instruction.quantity
  // Raw quantity for API calls (picking_qty in perform body)
  function effectiveQty(instruction) {
    if (instruction?.job_instruction_group_id && State.groupRecord?.units) {
      return State.groupRecord.units;
    }
    return instruction?.quantity ?? 1;
  }

  // Display quantity for UI and voice -- divides by UoM factor so picker sees
  // physical units (e.g. 18 eaches / factor 6 = 3 Cartons to pick)
  // For SIBP/MIBP groups, groupRecord.units is already in the correct display unit
  function displayQty(instruction) {
    if (instruction?.job_instruction_group_id && State.groupRecord?.units) {
      return State.groupRecord.units; // group qty is already display-ready
    }
    const raw    = instruction?.quantity ?? 1;
    const factor = instruction?.itemUnitOfMeasure?.factor || 1;
    if (factor <= 1) return raw;
    const divided = raw / factor;
    // Return integer if clean division, otherwise 2dp
    return Number.isInteger(divided) ? divided : parseFloat(divided.toFixed(2));
  }

  // Group-perform API call
  async function groupPerform(instruction, containerNo, pickingQty) {
    const groupId = instruction.job_instruction_group_id;
    const lastUpdatedAt = State.groupRecord?.updated_at;
    return apiPost(
      `job/job-instruction/group-perform&id=${groupId}`,
      {
        container_no:       containerNo,
        profile_id:         State.profile.id,
        container_type_id:  null,
        ship_no:            instruction.reference_number,
        is_tracking:        null,
        from_location:      instruction.from_location_id,
        item_id:            instruction.item_id,
        picking_qty:        pickingQty,
        container_location: null,
        group_id:           groupId,
        last_updated_at:    lastUpdatedAt,
      }
    );
  }


  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 6: CLUSTER PICK LOOP
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function resolveContainerForInstruction(instruction) {
    const pos = instruction?.cluster_position_id;
    if (!pos) return null;
    return State.containersByPosition[pos] || null;
  }

  function showMultiToteModal(containerNo, existingPositionId, newPositionId) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
      if (!screen) { resolve(false); return; }
      const overlay = document.createElement('div');
      overlay.className = 'mpk-modal-overlay';
      overlay.id = 'mpk-multitote-modal';
      overlay.innerHTML = `
        <div class="mpk-modal-card">
          <div class="mpk-modal-header">[!] Container already used</div>
          <div class="mpk-modal-body">
            <strong>${_esc(containerNo)}</strong> is assigned to Position ${_esc(String(existingPositionId))}.<br><br>
            Use it for Position ${_esc(String(newPositionId))} as well?
            <br><small style="color:#9faecb;margin-top:4px;display:block">Confirm only if picking multiple orders into the same tote.</small>
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-modal-actions">
            <button id="mpk-multitote-yes" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-primary">Yes - multi-tote pick</button>
            <button id="mpk-multitote-no"  class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">No - scan a different tote</button>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      screen.appendChild(overlay);
      document.getElementById('mpk-multitote-yes')?.addEventListener('click', () => { overlay.remove(); resolve(true); });
      document.getElementById('mpk-multitote-no')?.addEventListener('click',  () => { overlay.remove(); resolve(false); });
    });
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FRAGMENT 4: STANDARD PICK LOOP
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------


  // -- Item barcode verification (client-side) -------------------------------
  function verifyItem(barcode) {
    const key = barcode.trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!key) return false;

    const instr = State.instruction;
    if (!instr) return false;

    // Determine which UoM this instruction requires
    // instruction.itemUnitOfMeasure.id identifies the specific UoM to pick in
    const requiredUomId = instr.itemUnitOfMeasure?.id;

    if (requiredUomId) {
      // Find the matching UoM entry on the item
      const targetUom = (instr.item?.itemUnitOfMeasures || []).find(
        u => u.id === requiredUomId
      );

      if (targetUom) {
        const refs = (targetUom.itemUnitOfMeasureReference || []).map(
          r => r.reference?.toLowerCase()
        ).filter(Boolean);

        if (refs.length > 0) {
          // UoM has specific barcodes -- ONLY accept those, not other UoM barcodes
          // This prevents scanning an Each barcode when picking Cartons
          return refs.includes(key);
        }
        // UoM has no barcode references -- fall through to item_code fallback
      }
    }

    // Fallback: accept item_code (universal identifier, always scannable)
    if (instr.item?.item_code?.toLowerCase() === key) return true;

    return false;
  }

  // -- Fire-and-forget item verification API call -----------------------------
  function fireItemVerification(instruction, scannedBarcode) {
    const itemCode  = instruction.item?.item_code;
    const ref       = instruction.reference_number;
    const companyId = instruction.item?.company_id || 46;
    if (!itemCode || !ref) return;
    // item_code_use=Yes if picker scanned the item_code itself, No if a UoM reference
    const itemCodeUse = scannedBarcode &&
      scannedBarcode.trim().toLowerCase() === itemCode.toLowerCase() ? 'Yes' : 'No';
    const path = `configuration/item/process-log-item-verification` +
      `&item_code=${encodeURIComponent(itemCode)}` +
      `&reference=${encodeURIComponent(ref)}` +
      `&company_id=${companyId}` +
      `&item_code_use=${itemCodeUse}&screen=Picking&status=success`;
    apiGet(path).catch(e => console.warn('[MalpaPick] verification log failed:', e.message));
  }

  // -- Container label validation (client-side) ------------------------------
  function validateContainerLabel(label) {
    if (!label) return false;
    const upper = label.trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!upper) return false;
    // Use pre-built prefix list for O(1) lookup
    if (State.containerPrefixes.length === 0) {
      // Fallback: rebuild if somehow empty (e.g. opened mid-session)
      State.containerPrefixes = State.containerTypes
        .map(ct => (ct.container_number_prefix || '').toUpperCase())
        .filter(Boolean);
    }
    return State.containerPrefixes.some(prefix => upper.startsWith(prefix));
  }

  // -- Fetch next instruction - try cache first, then API -------------------
  async function fetchNextInstruction(hintInstruction) {
    // Try to find the full version in State.allInstructions by id
    if (hintInstruction?.id) {
      const cached = State.allInstructions.find(i => i.id === hintInstruction.id);
      if (cached?.fromLocation && cached?.item) return cached;
    }
    // Cache miss - fetch fresh from API with full expand
    const EXPAND = [
      'fromLocation', 'toLocation',
      'item.itemUnitOfMeasures.itemUnitOfMeasureReference',
      'item.itemUnitOfMeasures.unitOfMeasure',
      'batch', 'license_plate_no', 'shipmentNumber',
      'itemUnitOfMeasure.unitOfMeasure',
      'jobInstructionGroup.id',
      'shipmentDetailChildren', 'item.company', 'custom_field_1',
    ].join(',');
    let path = `shipment/shipment-picking-profile/get-job-instructions` +
      `&id=${State.profile.id}&expand=${encodeURIComponent(EXPAND)}`;
    if (State.jobId) path += `&job_id=${State.jobId}`;
    const data = await apiGet(path);
    const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
    return arr[0] || null;
  }

  // -- Perform pick API call -------------------------------------------------
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // LOCOD FLOW -- profile ID 54, auto_generate_container_check = 1
  // No tote scan required -- container is auto-generated by C7
  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

  const LOCOD_PROFILE_ID    = 54;
  const LOCOD_CONTAINER_TYPE = 38; // Pick Container - Auto (prefix AC)

  function isLocod() {
    return State.profile?.id === LOCOD_PROFILE_ID;
  }

  // Check if shipment already has an assigned container
  async function fetchPickingContainer(shipmentNumber) {
    try {
      const data = await apiGet(
        `shipment/shipment-container/get-picking-container` +
        `&shipmentNumber=${encodeURIComponent(shipmentNumber)}`
      );
      return data?.shipmentContainerNumber || null;
    } catch(e) {
      console.warn('[MalpaPick] get-picking-container failed:', e.message);
      return null;
    }
  }

  // Auto-generate a container number from C7
  async function autoGenerateContainerNumber() {
    const data = await apiGet(
      'shipment/shipment-container/auto-generate-container-number'
    );
    return data?.container_number || null;
  }

  // Fire label print -- fire-and-forget, never blocks the pick flow
  function printConsignmentLabel(instruction) {
    apiGet(
      `shipment/shipment-picking-profile/print-consignment-piece-label` +
      `&job_instruction_id=${instruction.id}` +
      `&item_id=${instruction.item_id}`
    ).catch(e => console.warn('[MalpaPick] print-label failed:', e.message));
  }

  // Full LOCOD pick -- called after item verified, bypasses container scan screen
  async function performLocodPick(instruction) {
    State.screen = 'TRANSITIONING';
    document.querySelector('.mpk-item-block')?.classList.add('verified');
    setScanFeedback('Processing...', 'dim');

    try {
      const pickingQty = effectiveQty(instruction);
      const shipNo     = instruction.reference_number;

      // Step 1: check for existing container + fire item verification in parallel
      const [existingContainer] = await Promise.all([
        fetchPickingContainer(shipNo),
        Promise.resolve(), // verification already fired on item scan
      ]);

      // Step 2: get or generate container number
      let containerNo = existingContainer;
      if (!containerNo) {
        containerNo = await autoGenerateContainerNumber();
      }
      if (!containerNo) throw new Error('Could not get container number');

      // Step 3: fire label print (non-blocking)
      printConsignmentLabel(instruction);

      // Step 4: perform with LOCOD-specific fields
      const _doLocod = () => apiPost(
        `job/job-instruction/perform&id=${instruction.id}`,
        {
          container_no:       containerNo,
          profile_id:         LOCOD_PROFILE_ID,
          container_type_id:  LOCOD_CONTAINER_TYPE,
          ship_no:            shipNo,
          is_tracking:        null,
          from_location:      instruction.from_location_id,
          item_id:            instruction.item_id,
          picking_qty:        pickingQty,
          container_location: null,
          selected_profile_id: LOCOD_PROFILE_ID,
        }
      );

      let result;
      try {
        result = await _doLocod();
      } catch(firstErr) {
        if (firstErr.message?.includes('Session expired')) throw firstErr;
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 800));
        result = await _doLocod();
      }

      // Success
      Audio.chime('container_ok');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([30]);
      if (State.pickProgress) State.pickProgress.current++;
      savePickResumeState();

      const completedId = instruction.id;
      const isJobDone   = result.job_instruction === null;

      if (result.job_instruction !== null) {
        changeSequence(completedId);
      }

      if (isJobDone) {
        renderJobComplete(false);
      } else {
        const fullNext = await fetchNextInstruction(result.job_instruction);
        const nextInstr = fullNext || result.job_instruction;
        State.instruction = nextInstr;
        State.jobId = nextInstr.job_id || State.jobId;
        await loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(nextInstr);
        renderPickScreen(nextInstr);
        setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(nextInstr, instruction), 150);
      }

    } catch(err) {
      State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';
      setScanFeedback(err.message || 'Error - try again', 'err');
      Audio.chime('error');
      Voice.error('Error, try again');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([60, 30, 60]);
      setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 100);
    }
  }

  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

  async function performPick(instruction, containerNo, pickingQty) {
    return apiPost(
      `job/job-instruction/perform&id=${instruction.id}`,
      {
        container_no:       containerNo,
        profile_id:         State.profile.id,
        container_type_id:  null,
        ship_no:            instruction.reference_number,
        is_tracking:        null,
        from_location:      instruction.from_location_id,
        item_id:            instruction.item_id,
        picking_qty:        pickingQty,
        container_location: null,
        selected_profile_id: State.profile?.id || null,
      }
    );
  }

  // -- Change sequence -------------------------------------------------------
  async function changeSequence(instructionId) {
    return apiGet(`shipment/shipment-picking-profile/change-sequence&id=${instructionId}`).catch(
      e => console.warn('[MalpaPick] change-sequence failed:', e.message)
    );
  }

  // -- Pick state machine ----------------------------------------------------
  // States: PICK_ITEM -> PICK_QTY_MODAL (qty>1) -> SCAN_CONTAINER -> (loop or complete)

  function onItemScan(barcode) {
    if (!verifyItem(barcode)) {
      setScanFeedback('Wrong item - scan again', 'err');
      Audio.chime('error');
      Voice.error('Wrong item');
      return;
    }

    const qty = effectiveQty(State.instruction);

    if (qty === 1) {
      setScanFeedback('Item verified v', 'ok');
      Audio.chime('item_done');
      fireItemVerification(State.instruction, barcode);
      State.scanCount = 1;
      State.screen = 'TRANSITIONING';

      if (isLocod()) {
        // LOCOD: auto-generate container, no tote scan needed
        performLocodPick(State.instruction);
      } else {
        document.querySelector('.mpk-item-block')?.classList.add('verified');
        const clusterPosNow = State.instruction?.cluster_position_id;
        if (clusterPosNow) {
          Voice.announcePosition(clusterPosNow);
          setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 600);
        } else {
          setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 150);
        }
        setTimeout(() => renderContainerScan(), 500);
      }
    } else {
      // Multiple units - show qty modal
      State.scanCount = 1;
      Audio.chime('item_done');
      renderQtyModal();
    }
  }

  // -- Container scan screen -------------------------------------------------
  function renderContainerScan() {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;
    State.screen = 'SCAN_CONTAINER';

    const clusterPos = State.instruction?.cluster_position_id;
    const existingContainer = clusterPos ? State.containersByPosition[clusterPos] : null;

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-pick-screen" id="mpk-pick-screen">
        <div class="mpk-loc-header">
          <div class="mpk-loc-header-top">
            <span class="mpk-loc-label">${State.instruction?.cluster_position_id ? `Pos ${State.instruction.cluster_position_id} - Scan Container` : 'Scan Container'}</span>
            <span class="mpk-loc-progress-text">${State.pickProgress?.current || 1} / ${State.pickProgress?.total || '?'} instructions</span>
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-loc-code">${_esc(State.instruction?.fromLocation?.location_code || '-')}</div>
          <div class="mpk-progress-track">
            <div class="mpk-progress-fill" style="width:${State.pickProgress?.total ? Math.round(((State.pickProgress.current-1)/State.pickProgress.total)*100) : 0}%"></div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-item-block verified">
          <div class="mpk-qty-label">Picked</div>
          <div class="mpk-qty-value" style="color:#79c447">${State.scanCount}</div>
          <div class="mpk-item-sku">${_esc(State.instruction?.item?.item_code || '-')}</div>
          <div class="mpk-item-desc">${_esc(State.instruction?.item?.abc_category || State.instruction?.item?.description || '')}</div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-scan-area">
          <div class="mpk-scan-zone" id="mpk-scan-zone">
            <div class="mpk-scan-zone-label" style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700">SCAN TOTE NOW</div>
            ${existingContainer ? `<div style="font-size:11px;color:#20a8d8;font-weight:600;margin-top:2px">Last used: ${_esc(existingContainer)}</div>` : ''}
            <div class="mpk-scan-arrows">&gt;&gt;&gt;</div>
            <input id="mpk-scan-in" type="text" inputmode="none"
              autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false"/>
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-scan-feedback dim" id="mpk-scan-fb">Ready to scan</div>
        </div>

        <div class="mpk-cluster-strip${clusterPos ? ' visible' : ''}" id="mpk-cluster-strip">
          <span class="mpk-cluster-pos-badge">${clusterPos ?? ''}</span>
          <span class="mpk-cluster-pos-label">Position ${clusterPos ?? ''}</span>
          <span class="mpk-cluster-container${existingContainer ? ' assigned' : ''}" id="mpk-cluster-container">${existingContainer ? _esc(existingContainer) : 'No tote yet'}</span>
        </div>

      </div>
      <div class="mpk-pick-actions">
        <button id="mpk-back-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-secondary">&lt;- Back</button>
      </div>`;

    R.scanIn = document.getElementById('mpk-scan-in');
    R.scanFb = document.getElementById('mpk-scan-fb');
    document.getElementById('mpk-back-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      State.scanCount = 0;
      renderPickScreen(State.instruction);
    });

    if (R.scanIn) {
      R.scanIn.addEventListener('keydown', _onScanKeydown);
      // Longer delay - confirm button may hold focus briefly
      setTimeout(() => { R.scanIn?.focus(); }, 200);
