    }

    // If cluster pos already has a container, auto-pre-fill hint
    if (existingContainer) State._pendingContainer = existingContainer;
  }

  async function onContainerScan(containerNo) {
    const label = containerNo.trim();

    // Client-side prefix validation
    if (!validateContainerLabel(label)) {
      setScanFeedback('Tote does not exist', 'err');
      Audio.chime('error');
      Voice.error('Wrong tote');
      return;
    }

    const clusterPos = State.instruction?.cluster_position_id;

    // Cluster: check if container already assigned to a DIFFERENT position
    if (clusterPos && State.containersByPosition) {
      const conflictPos = Object.keys(State.containersByPosition).find(
        pos => String(pos) !== String(clusterPos) &&
               State.containersByPosition[pos]?.toUpperCase() === label.toUpperCase()
      );
      if (conflictPos) {
        const proceed = await showMultiToteModal(label, conflictPos, clusterPos);
        if (!proceed) {
          setScanFeedback('Scan a different container', 'dim');
          setTimeout(() => { if (R.scanIn) { R.scanIn.disabled = false; R.scanIn.focus(); } }, 100);
          return;
        }
      }
    }

    if (R.scanIn) R.scanIn.disabled = true;
    setScanFeedback('Confirming?', 'dim');

    try {
      const pickQty = State.scanCount || effectiveQty(State.instruction);
      const _doPerform = () => State.instruction.job_instruction_group_id
        ? groupPerform(State.instruction, label, pickQty)
        : performPick(State.instruction, label, pickQty);
      let result;
      try {
        result = await _doPerform();
      } catch (firstErr) {
        if (firstErr.message?.includes('Session expired')) throw firstErr;
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 800));
        result = await _doPerform();
      }

      // Success
      Audio.chime('container_ok');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([30]);

      if (clusterPos) {
        State.containersByPosition[clusterPos] = label;
        const stripCont = document.getElementById('mpk-cluster-container');
        if (stripCont) { stripCont.textContent = label; stripCont.classList.add('assigned'); }
      }

      const completedId = State.instruction.id;

      // Advance progress
      if (State.pickProgress) State.pickProgress.current++;

      // Save resume state after each completed pick
      savePickResumeState();

      // change-sequence only when NOT the final pick
      if (result.job_instruction !== null) {
        changeSequence(completedId);
      }

      // Check completion
      const isClusterDone = result.is_cluster_job === true && result.job_instruction === null;
      const isJobDone     = result.job_instruction === null;

      if (isJobDone) {
        // Announce completion - no next instruction to load
        if (clusterPos) Voice.announcePosition(clusterPos);
        renderJobComplete(isClusterDone);
      } else {
        // Resolve full next instruction + group record first
        const fullNext  = await fetchNextInstruction(result.job_instruction);
        const nextInstr = fullNext || result.job_instruction;
        State.instruction = nextInstr;
        State.jobId = nextInstr.job_id || State.jobId;
        await loadGroupRecordIfNeeded(nextInstr);

        // Now announce with correct qty (groupRecord loaded for SIBP/MIBP)
        // Cluster: announce position first, then after a beat announce next location
        if (clusterPos) {
          Voice.announcePosition(clusterPos);
          setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(nextInstr), 900);
        }

        renderPickScreen(nextInstr);
        // Announce AFTER render - prevents Voice.cancel() in renderPickScreen killing it
        if (clusterPos) {
          setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(nextInstr, State.instruction), 200);
        } else {
          setTimeout(() => Voice.announceInstruction(nextInstr, State.instruction), 150);
        }
      }

    } catch (err) {
      if (R.scanIn) R.scanIn.disabled = false;

      // Container conflict (code 1022)
      if (err.message?.includes('belongs to another shipment') || err.message?.includes('1022')) {
        setScanFeedback('Container belongs to another shipment', 'err');
        Voice.error('Wrong tote');
      } else {
        setScanFeedback(err.message || 'Error - try again', 'err');
        Voice.error('Error, try again');
      }
      Audio.chime('error');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([60, 30, 60]);
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (R.scanIn) { R.scanIn.disabled = false; R.scanIn?.focus(); }
      }, 100);
    }
  }

  // -- Qty numpad overlay (floats over pick screen) -------------------------
  function renderQtyModal() {
    State.screen = 'QTY_MODAL';
    // Remove any existing overlay
    document.getElementById('mpk-numpad-overlay')?.remove();

    const screen = document.getElementById('mpk-pick-screen');
    if (!screen) return;

    let entered = '';
    let _firstKey = true;

    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'mpk-numpad-overlay';
    overlay.id = 'mpk-numpad-overlay';

    const render = () => {
      const requiredQty = displayQty(State.instruction);
      // Default display: 1 (picker has scanned 1 item to trigger the modal)
      // Shows the required qty as a target hint below
      const display = entered || '1';
      overlay.innerHTML = `
        <div class="mpk-numpad-sheet">
          <div class="mpk-numpad-display">
            ${_esc(display)}
            <span class="mpk-numpad-target">of ${requiredQty} required</span>
          </div>
          <div class="mpk-numpad-grid">
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="1">1</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="2">2</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="3">3</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="4">4</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="5">5</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="6">6</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="7">7</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="8">8</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="9">9</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key cancel" data-k="cancel">X</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key" data-k="0">0</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key del" data-k="del">&lt;-</button>
            <button class="mpk-numpad-key confirm" data-k="confirm">Confirm ${_esc(display)}</button>
          </div>
        </div>`;

      overlay.querySelectorAll('.mpk-numpad-key').forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', e => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          const k = btn.dataset.k;
          if (k === 'cancel') {
            overlay.remove();
            State.screen = 'PICK_ITEM';
            State.scanCount = 0;
          } else if (k === 'del') {
            entered = entered.slice(0, -1);
            _firstKey = entered.length === 0;
            render();
          } else if (k === 'confirm') {
            let val = entered ? parseInt(entered, 10) : 1;
            if (!val || val < 1) return;
            if (val > requiredQty) val = requiredQty; // final guard -- never exceed
            overlay.remove();
            State.scanCount = val;
            fireItemVerification(State.instruction);
            if (isLocod()) {
              performLocodPick(State.instruction);
            } else {
              document.querySelector('.mpk-item-block')?.classList.add('verified');
              const _cPos = State.instruction?.cluster_position_id;
              if (_cPos) {
                Voice.announcePosition(_cPos);
                setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 600);
              } else {
                setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 150);
              }
              setTimeout(() => renderContainerScan(), 300);
            }
          } else {
            let candidate;
            if (_firstKey) { candidate = k; }
            else if (entered.length < 4) { candidate = entered + k; }
            else { candidate = entered; }

            // Cap at required qty -- block digits that would exceed it
            const candidateVal = parseInt(candidate, 10);
            if (!isNaN(candidateVal) && candidateVal > requiredQty) {
              // Snap to the max allowed instead of silently ignoring the tap
              entered = String(requiredQty);
            } else {
              entered = candidate;
            }
            _firstKey = false;
            render();
          }
        });
      });
    };

    render();
    // Expose render fn so onQtyModalScan can sync the display
    overlay._rerender = (newCount) => {
      entered = String(newCount);
      render();
    };
    screen.appendChild(overlay);

    // Re-focus hidden scan input so scanner can still increment by scanning
    setTimeout(() => R.scanIn?.focus(), 100);
  }

  // Called when scanning additional items while numpad overlay is open
  function onQtyModalScan(barcode) {
    const qty = effectiveQty(State.instruction);

    // Block further scans once target reached -- prevents overscan
    if (State.scanCount >= qty) {
      setScanFeedback('Target already reached', 'dim');
      return;
    }

    if (!verifyItem(barcode)) {
      Audio.chime('error');
      Voice.error('Wrong item');
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([60, 30, 60]);
      return;
    }

    State.scanCount++;
    Audio.chime('item_done');

    // Sync the numpad display via the exposed rerender function
    const overlay = document.getElementById('mpk-numpad-overlay');
    if (overlay?._rerender) {
      overlay._rerender(State.scanCount);
    }

    if (State.scanCount >= qty) {
      // All scanned - auto-confirm after brief pause
      Audio.chime('item_done');
      fireItemVerification(State.instruction);
      overlay?.remove();
      if (isLocod()) {
        performLocodPick(State.instruction);
      } else {
        document.querySelector('.mpk-item-block')?.classList.add('verified');
        const clusterPosMod = State.instruction?.cluster_position_id;
        if (clusterPosMod) {
          Voice.announcePosition(clusterPosMod);
          setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 600);
        } else {
          setTimeout(() => Voice.speak('Scan tote'), 150);
        }
        setTimeout(() => renderContainerScan(), 400);
      }
    }
  }

  // -- Job complete screen ---------------------------------------------------
  function renderJobComplete(isCluster) {
    const root = document.getElementById('mpk-root');
    if (!root) return;
    State.screen = 'JOB_COMPLETE';
    clearPickResumeState(); // job done - no need to resume

    const total = State.pickProgress?.total || '?';

    root.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mpk-screen">
        <div class="mpk-screen-header">Job Complete</div>
        <div class="mpk-screen-body" style="align-items:center;justify-content:center;text-align:center;gap:12px">
          <div style="font-size:56px;line-height:1">v</div>
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:700;color:#79c447">
            ${isCluster ? 'Cluster complete' : 'Job complete'}
          </div>
          <div style="font-size:14px;color:#9faecb">${total} instructions picked</div>
          <div style="font-size:13px;color:#9faecb;margin-top:4px">${_esc(State.profile?.name || '')}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="mpk-spacer"></div>
      <div class="mpk-btn-stack">
        <button id="mpk-newjob-btn" class="mpk-btn mpk-btn-primary">Start Next Job</button>
      </div>`;

    Voice.speak(isCluster ? 'Cluster complete' : 'Job complete');
    Audio.chime('container_ok');
    if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([30, 50, 30, 50, 60]);

    document.getElementById('mpk-newjob-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      State.reset();
      renderProfileSelect();
    });
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // FOCUS RECOVERY -- keeps scan input focused on TC51 after sleep/notification
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  const _SCAN_SCREENS = ['PICK_ITEM', 'SCAN_CONTAINER', 'QTY_MODAL', 'SHORT_PICK_LOCATION'];

  function _refocusScanInput() {
    if (!_SCAN_SCREENS.includes(State.screen)) return;
    // Route to the correct input for the current screen
    const inputId = State.screen === 'SHORT_PICK_LOCATION' ? 'mpk-sp-scan-in' : 'mpk-scan-in';
    const el = document.getElementById(inputId);
    if (!el || !document.contains(el)) return;
    if (document.activeElement === el) return;
    el.focus();
    if (inputId === 'mpk-scan-in') R.scanIn = el; // refresh stale ref
  }

  // A. Page becomes visible (screen wake, app foreground)
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') setTimeout(_refocusScanInput, 300);
  });

  // B. Window regains focus (notification dismissed, overlay closed)
  window.addEventListener('focus', () => {
    setTimeout(_refocusScanInput, 200);
  });

  // C. Periodic poll every 2.5s -- catches anything missed by A and B
  setInterval(() => {
    if (!document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view')) return; // tab not open
    _refocusScanInput();
  }, 2500);

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 6. CLOSE UI
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function closeUI() {
    // Unassign job if picker closes during summary (job assigned but not accepted)
    const preAcceptScreens = ['JOB_SUMMARY', 'JOB_NUM_ENTRY'];
    const activePickScreens = ['PICK_ITEM','SCAN_CONTAINER','QTY_MODAL','TRANSITIONING',
                                'SHORT_PICK_LOCATION','SHORT_PICK_REASON'];
    if (preAcceptScreens.includes(State.screen) && State.jobId) {
      unassignJob(State.jobId);
      clearPickResumeState();
    } else if (activePickScreens.includes(State.screen) && State.jobId) {
      // Mid-pick close - save resume state so picker can continue on re-open
      savePickResumeState();
    } else {
      clearPickResumeState();
    }
    document.removeEventListener('keydown', onGlobalKey);
    window.removeEventListener('resize', measureHeight);

    // Restore sidebar to its previous state
    if (!R._sidebarWasMinimized) document.body.classList.remove('sidebar-minimized');
    if (!R._brandWasMinimized)   document.body.classList.remove('brand-minimized');

    document.getElementById('mpk-tab-li')?.remove();
    document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view')?.remove();

    // Restore exactly the tab + panel that were active before we opened
    if (R._prevActiveLi && document.contains(R._prevActiveLi)) {
      R._prevActiveLi.classList.add('active');
      const a = R._prevActiveLi.querySelector('a.nav-link');
      if (a) { a.classList.add('active'); a.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true'); }
    } else {
      // Fallback: activate last tab in the bar
      const tabBar = document.querySelector('ul.nav.nav-tabs[role="tablist"]');
      if (tabBar) {
        const lastLi = Array.from(tabBar.querySelectorAll('li.nav-item')).pop();
        if (lastLi) {
          lastLi.classList.add('active');
          const a = lastLi.querySelector('a.nav-link');
          if (a) { a.classList.add('active'); a.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true'); }
        }
      }
    }

    if (R._prevActivePanel && document.contains(R._prevActivePanel)) {
      R._prevActivePanel.classList.add('active');
      R._prevActivePanel.style.display = '';
    } else {
      // Fallback: show last panel
      const tabContent = document.querySelector('div.tab-content');
      if (tabContent) {
        const panels = Array.from(tabContent.querySelectorAll(':scope > tab, :scope > .tab-pane'));
        if (panels.length) {
          const last = panels[panels.length - 1];
          last.classList.add('active');
          last.style.display = '';
        }
      }
    }

    State.reset();
    R = {};
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 7. KEYBOARD
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function onGlobalKey(e) {
    if (!document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view')) return;
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeUI();
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 8. OPEN PICK (entry point from nav click)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  function openPick() {
    if (document.getElementById('mpk-tab-view')) return; // already open
    try {
      injectCSS();
      buildShell();
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[MalpaPick] openPick error:', err);
      // Surface error visibly even without DevTools
      const errDiv = document.createElement('div');
      errDiv.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:80px;left:210px;right:20px;z-index:99999;background:#7f1d1d;color:#fff;padding:16px 20px;border-radius:6px;font-family:monospace;font-size:13px;white-space:pre-wrap;';
      errDiv.textContent = '[MalpaPick Error] ' + err.message + '\n\n' + err.stack;
      const cls = document.createElement('button');
      cls.textContent = 'x';
      cls.style.cssText = 'float:right;background:none;border:none;color:#fff;font-size:20px;cursor:pointer;margin:-4px -4px 0 0;';
      cls.onclick = () => errDiv.remove();
      errDiv.prepend(cls);
      document.body.appendChild(errDiv);
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // 9. BOOT
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  // Capture session ID as early as possible (XHR intercept)
  // Pre-warm session ID capture at boot - by the time user taps nav it's resolved
  captureSessionId();
  // Start polling immediately so _sessionId is ready before first API call
  (async () => {
    for (let i = 0; i < 50 && !_sessionId; i++) {
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
      captureSessionId();
    }
  })();

  // Retry injecting nav until C7's Angular sidebar has rendered
  let _attempts = 0;
  function tryInject() {
    if (document.querySelector('div.sidebar nav li.nav-item')) {
      injectCSS();
      injectNav();
      return;
    }
    if (++_attempts < 80) setTimeout(tryInject, 500);
  }

  // MutationObserver: re-inject nav if Angular tears it down and rebuilds the sidebar
  new MutationObserver(() => {
    if (
      !document.getElementById('mpk-nav') &&
      document.querySelector('div.sidebar nav li.nav-item')
    ) {
      injectNav();
    }
  }).observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });

  tryInject();

})();
